```python
"""
Chemical Inventory Service Layer
Business logic for chemical inventory operations
"""
import os
from sqlalchemy import create_engine, text
from dotenv import load_dotenv

from flask import current_app

_chem_engine = None

def get_chem_engine():
    """Create or return the global chemical database engine"""
    global _chem_engine
    if _chem_engine is None:
        try:
            # Prefer Flask's app context if available
            host = current_app.config.get("CHEM_PGHOST", "localhost")
            port = current_app.config.get("CHEM_PGPORT", "5432")
            db = current_app.config.get("CHEM_POSTGRES_DB", "cheminventory")
            user = current_app.config.get("CHEM_POSTGRES_USER", "postgres")
            pwd = current_app.config.get("CHEM_POSTGRES_PASSWORD", "changeme")
        except RuntimeError:
            # Fallback for offline scripts or missing context
            load_dotenv()
            host = os.getenv("CHEM_PGHOST", os.getenv("PGHOST", "localhost"))
            port = os.getenv("CHEM_PGPORT", os.getenv("PGPORT", "5432"))
            db = os.getenv("CHEM_POSTGRES_DB", os.getenv("POSTGRES_DB", "cheminventory"))
            user = os.getenv("CHEM_POSTGRES_USER", os.getenv("POSTGRES_USER", "postgres"))
            pwd = os.getenv("CHEM_POSTGRES_PASSWORD", os.getenv("POSTGRES_PASSWORD", "changeme"))

        url = f"postgresql+psycopg2://{user}:{pwd}@{host}:{port}/{db}"
        # Maintain a persistent pool that tests connections on checkout (pre-ping)
        _chem_engine = create_engine(url, pool_pre_ping=True, pool_size=5, max_overflow=10, future=True)

    return _chem_engine


class ChemInventoryService:
    """Service for chemical inventory operations"""

    def __init__(self):
        """Initialize with database engine"""
        self.engine = get_chem_engine()

    # -------------------------
    # Helper Methods
    # -------------------------

    def _upsert(self, conn, table, key_col, value, id_col=None):
        """Insert or get existing record by unique column"""
        if value is None or str(value).strip() == "":
            return None

        if id_col is None:
            id_map = {
                "categories": "category_id",
                "vendors": "vendor_id",
                "rooms": "room_id",
                "items": "item_id",
                "containers": "container_id",
            }
            id_col = id_map.get(table, f"{table[:-1]}_id")

        val = str(value).strip()
        row = conn.execute(
            text(f"SELECT {id_col} FROM {table} WHERE {key_col}=:v"),
            {"v": val}
        ).fetchone()

        if row:
            return row[0]

        return conn.execute(
            text(f"INSERT INTO {table}({key_col}) VALUES (:v) RETURNING {id_col}"),
            {"v": val}
        ).scalar()

    def _next_barcode(self, conn):
        """Generate next barcode from sequence"""
        return str(conn.execute(text("SELECT nextval('seq_barcode')")).scalar())

#Resolve room updated 4/15/2026 for add templates
    def _resolve_room(self, conn, room_no, room_desc, area_class, room_name=None):
        print("USING _resolve_room WRAPPER")
        return self.resolve_room_id(
            conn,
            room_no=room_no,
            room_desc=room_desc or room_name,
            area_class=area_class,
        )
#Added 4/15/2026 Resolve room id fix function to work with templates
    def resolve_room_id(self, conn, room_no=None, room_desc=None, area_class=None):
        from sqlalchemy import text
        print("USING resolve_room_id")
        def clean_str(value):
            if value is None:
                return None
            value = str(value).strip()
            return value if value else None

        room_no = clean_str(room_no)
        room_desc = clean_str(room_desc)
        area_class = clean_str(area_class)

        print("USING NEW RESOLVE_ROOM_ID", room_no, room_desc, area_class)

        if not room_no and not room_desc and not area_class:
            return None

        # 1) Prefer exact room_no match
        if room_no:
            found = conn.execute(
                text("""
                    SELECT room_id
                    FROM rooms
                    WHERE room_no = :room_no
                    LIMIT 1
                """),
                {"room_no": room_no}
            ).mappings().first()

            if found:
                room_id = found["room_id"]

                conn.execute(
                    text("""
                        UPDATE rooms
                        SET
                            room_desc = COALESCE(:room_desc, room_desc),
                            area_class = COALESCE(:area_class, area_class)
                        WHERE room_id = :room_id
                    """),
                    {
                        "room_id": room_id,
                        "room_desc": room_desc,
                        "area_class": area_class,
                    }
                )
                return room_id

        # 2) Then try exact room_desc
        if room_desc:
            found = conn.execute(
                text("""
                    SELECT room_id
                    FROM rooms
                    WHERE room_desc = :room_desc
                    LIMIT 1
                """),
                {"room_desc": room_desc}
            ).mappings().first()

            if found:
                return found["room_id"]

        # 3) Then try exact room_name
        if room_desc:
            found = conn.execute(
                text("""
                    SELECT room_id
                    FROM rooms
                    WHERE room_name = :room_name
                    LIMIT 1
                """),
                {"room_name": room_desc}
            ).mappings().first()

            if found:
                return found["room_id"]

        # 4) Safe upsert by room_no
        if room_no:
            room_name = room_desc or room_no or "Unknown"

            row = conn.execute(
                text("""
                    INSERT INTO rooms (room_no, room_name, room_desc, area_class)
                    VALUES (:room_no, :room_name, :room_desc, :area_class)
                    ON CONFLICT (room_no)
                    DO UPDATE SET
                        room_desc = COALESCE(EXCLUDED.room_desc, rooms.room_desc),
                        area_class = COALESCE(EXCLUDED.area_class, rooms.area_class)
                    RETURNING room_id
                """),
                {
                    "room_no": room_no,
                    "room_name": room_name,
                    "room_desc": room_desc,
                    "area_class": area_class,
                }
            ).mappings().first()

            return row["room_id"] if row else None

        # 5) Last fallback: create room without room_no
        room_name = room_desc or "Unknown"

        row = conn.execute(
            text("""
                INSERT INTO rooms (room_no, room_name, room_desc, area_class)
                VALUES (:room_no, :room_name, :room_desc, :area_class)
                RETURNING room_id
            """),
            {
                "room_no": None,
                "room_name": room_name,
                "room_desc": room_desc,
                "area_class": area_class,
            }
        ).mappings().first()

        return row["room_id"] if row else None

#New search Inventory 4/15/2026 fixed show remove error UPDATED 4/20/2026
    def search_inventory(self, query="", limit=500, show_removed=False):
        from sqlalchemy import text

        q = (query or "").strip()
        like = f"%{q}%"

        sql = """
            SELECT
                c.container_id,
                c.item_id,
                c.room_id,
                c.area_class,
                c.storage_location,
                c.storage_sublocation,
                c.storage_device,
                c.entry_date AS entry_date,
                c.entry_date AS inv_date,
                c.manuf_date,
                c.expiry_date AS exp_date,
                c.lot_number,
                c.choice,
                c.nmr,
                c.nmr_expiry,
                c.owner,
                c.notes,
                c.added_by,
                c.barcode,
                c.size,
                c.unit,
                c.system,
                c.status,
                c.created_at,
                c.last_scan_at AS scan_date,
                i.name,
                i.catalog_number,
                i.physical_state,
                v.vendor_name AS vendor,
                r.room_no,
                r.room_name
            FROM containers c
            LEFT JOIN items i ON c.item_id = i.item_id
            LEFT JOIN vendors v ON i.vendor_id = v.vendor_id
            LEFT JOIN rooms r ON c.room_id = r.room_id
            WHERE 1=1
        """

        params = {"limit": limit}

        if not show_removed:
            sql += " AND COALESCE(c.status, 'ACTIVE') != 'REMOVED' "

        if q:
            sql += """
                AND (
                    COALESCE(i.name, '') ILIKE :like
                    OR COALESCE(i.catalog_number, '') ILIKE :like
                    OR COALESCE(v.vendor_name, '') ILIKE :like
                    OR COALESCE(c.barcode, '') ILIKE :like
                    OR COALESCE(c.lot_number, '') ILIKE :like
                    OR COALESCE(c.owner, '') ILIKE :like
                    OR COALESCE(c.system, '') ILIKE :like
                    OR COALESCE(c.storage_location, '') ILIKE :like
                    OR COALESCE(c.storage_sublocation, '') ILIKE :like
                    OR COALESCE(c.storage_device, '') ILIKE :like
                    OR COALESCE(r.room_no, '') ILIKE :like
                    OR COALESCE(r.room_name, '') ILIKE :like
                    OR COALESCE(c.notes, '') ILIKE :like
                )
            """
            params["like"] = like

        sql += """
            ORDER BY
                i.name NULLS LAST,
                c.barcode NULLS LAST
            LIMIT :limit
        """

        with self.engine.begin() as conn:
            rows = conn.execute(text(sql), params).mappings().all()

        return rows

#ADD CONTAINER UPDATED 4/16/2026
    def add_containers(self, data):
        """Add new chemical containers - returns list of new barcodes"""
        with self.engine.begin() as conn:
            # Ensure default category exists
            conn.execute(text("""
                CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS categories (
                    category_id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
                    name TEXT UNIQUE
                )
            """))
            cat_id = self._upsert(conn, "categories", "name", "Chemicals")
            vendor_id = self._upsert(conn, "vendors", "vendor_name", data['vendor_name']) if data['vendor_name'] else None

            #UPDATED 4/15/2026 Room - now with room_name support
            room_id = self.resolve_room_id(
                conn,
                data.get("room_no"),
                data.get("room_desc") or data.get("room_name"),
                data.get("area_class"),
            )

            # Upsert item by NAME (unique); fill optional fields if missing
            item_id = conn.execute(text("""
                INSERT INTO items(name, description, catalog_number, physical_state, volume_size, vendor_id, category_id)
                VALUES (:n, :n, :c, :s, :sz, :vid, :cat)
                ON CONFLICT (name) DO UPDATE
                    SET vendor_id      = COALESCE(items.vendor_id,      EXCLUDED.vendor_id),
                        category_id    = COALESCE(items.category_id,    EXCLUDED.category_id),
                        catalog_number = COALESCE(items.catalog_number, EXCLUDED.catalog_number),
                        physical_state = COALESCE(items.physical_state, EXCLUDED.physical_state),
                        volume_size    = COALESCE(items.volume_size,    EXCLUDED.volume_size)
                RETURNING item_id
            """), {
                "n": data['name'],
                "c": data['catalog'] or None,
                "s": data['state'] or None,
                "sz": data['size'] or None,
                "vid": vendor_id,
                "cat": cat_id
            }).scalar()
            # Create N containers with unique barcodes
            qty = data.get('qty', 1)
            new_barcodes = []

            for _ in range(qty):
                bc = self._next_barcode(conn)
                new_barcodes.append(bc)

                result = conn.execute(text("""
                    INSERT INTO containers(
                        item_id, barcode, container_code,
                        room_id, entry_date, manuf_date, expiry_date,
                        area_class, storage_location, storage_sublocation, storage_device,
                        system, lot_number, choice, nmr, nmr_expiry,
                        owner, notes, status, size, unit, added_by
                    ) VALUES (
                        :item, :bc, :bc,
                        :room, :entry, :manuf, :exp,
                        :ac, :sloc, :ssub, :sdev,
                        :sys, :lot, :choice, :nmr, :nmr_exp,
                        :owner, :notes, 'Active', :sz, :u, :added_by
                    )
                    RETURNING container_id
                """), {
                    "item": item_id,
                    "bc": bc,
                    "room": room_id,
                    "entry": data['entry'],
                    "manuf": data['manuf_date'],
                    "exp": data['expire'],
                    "ac": data['area_class'] or None,
                    "sloc": data['storage_location'] or None,
                    "ssub": data['storage_subloc'] or None,
                    "sdev": data['storage_device'] or None,
                    "sys": data['system'] or None,
                    "lot": data['lot_number'] or None,
                    "choice": data['choice'] or None,
                    "nmr": data['nmr'] or None,
                    "nmr_exp": data['nmr_exp'],
                    "owner": data['owner'] or None,
                    "notes": data['notes'] or None,
                    "sz": data['size'] or None,
                    "u": data['unit'] or None,
                    "added_by": data.get('added_by') or None
                })

                container_id = result.scalar()

                self.log_transaction(
                    conn,
                    action="ADD",
                    container_id=container_id,
                    barcode=bc,
                    item_id=item_id,
                    room_id=room_id,
                    performed_by=data.get("added_by") or None,
                    details={
                        "lot_number": data.get("lot_number") or None,
                        "owner": data.get("owner") or None,
                        "storage_location": data.get("storage_location") or None,
                        "storage_sublocation": data.get("storage_subloc") or None,
                        "storage_device": data.get("storage_device") or None,
                        "size": data.get("size") or None,
                        "unit": data.get("unit") or None,
                        "notes": data.get("notes") or None
                    }
                )

            return new_barcodes


    def get_reports(self):
        """Get comprehensive inventory reports"""
        with self.engine.begin() as conn:
            # Totals
            totals = conn.execute(text("""
                SELECT
                    COUNT(*)                                           AS total_containers,
                    COUNT(DISTINCT material_name)                      AS unique_materials,
                    COUNT(*) FILTER (WHERE exp_date < CURRENT_DATE)    AS expired,
                    COUNT(*) FILTER (WHERE exp_date >= CURRENT_DATE
                                    AND exp_date < CURRENT_DATE + INTERVAL '30 days') AS expiring_30
                FROM inventory_view
            """)).mappings().one()

            # Expiring soon
            expiring = conn.execute(text("""
                SELECT * FROM inventory_view
                WHERE exp_date >= CURRENT_DATE
                    AND exp_date <  CURRENT_DATE + INTERVAL '30 days'
                ORDER BY exp_date, material_name
                LIMIT 1000
            """)).mappings().all()

            # Expired
            expired = conn.execute(text("""
                SELECT * FROM inventory_view
                WHERE exp_date < CURRENT_DATE
                ORDER BY exp_date DESC, material_name
                LIMIT 1000
            """)).mappings().all()

            # NMR due
            nmr_due = conn.execute(text("""
                SELECT * FROM inventory_view
                WHERE nmr_exp IS NOT NULL
                    AND nmr_exp < CURRENT_DATE + INTERVAL '30 days'
                ORDER BY nmr_exp, material_name
                LIMIT 1000
            """)).mappings().all()

            # By room
            by_room = conn.execute(text("""
                SELECT COALESCE(room_no,'(none)') AS room_no,
                        COALESCE(room_desc,'')     AS room_desc,
                        COUNT(*) AS n
                FROM inventory_view
                GROUP BY room_no, room_desc
                ORDER BY room_no NULLS FIRST, room_desc
            """)).mappings().all()

            # By vendor
            by_vendor = conn.execute(text("""
                SELECT COALESCE(vendor,'(none)') AS vendor, COUNT(*) AS n
                FROM inventory_view
                GROUP BY vendor
                ORDER BY n DESC, vendor
            """)).mappings().all()

            # By system
            by_system = conn.execute(text("""
                SELECT COALESCE(system,'(none)') AS system, COUNT(*) AS n
                FROM inventory_view
                GROUP BY system
                ORDER BY n DESC, system
            """)).mappings().all()

            # By owner
            by_owner = conn.execute(text("""
                SELECT COALESCE(owner,'(none)') AS owner, COUNT(*) AS n
                FROM inventory_view
                GROUP BY owner
                ORDER BY n DESC, owner
            """)).mappings().all()

        return {
            'totals': totals,
            'expiring': expiring,
            'expired': expired,
            'nmr_due': nmr_due,
            'by_room': by_room,
            'by_vendor': by_vendor,
            'by_system': by_system,
            'by_owner': by_owner,
        }
#Updated Import Scans 4/15/2026
    def import_scans(self, barcodes, filename=None, performed_by=None, report_name=None, location=None):
        from sqlalchemy import text

        cleaned = [b.strip() for b in barcodes if b and b.strip()]
        total = len(cleaned)

        with self.engine.begin() as conn:
            cycle_row = conn.execute(text("""
                INSERT INTO inventory_cycles (
                    filename,
                    performed_by,
                    report_name,
                    location,
                    total_scanned
                )
                VALUES (
                    :filename,
                    :performed_by,
                    :report_name,
                    :location,
                    :total_scanned
                )
                RETURNING cycle_id
            """), {
                "filename": filename,
                "performed_by": performed_by,
                "report_name": report_name,
                "location": location,
                "total_scanned": total
            }).fetchone()

            cycle_id = cycle_row[0]

            matched = 0
            unmatched = 0

            for barcode in cleaned:
                container = conn.execute(text("""
                    SELECT container_id
                    FROM containers
                    WHERE barcode = :barcode
                    LIMIT 1
                """), {"barcode": barcode}).fetchone()

                matched_container_id = container[0] if container else None
#updated scan upload 4/15/2026
                conn.execute(text("""
                    INSERT INTO scan_raw (
                        cycle_id,
                        raw_code,
                        barcode,
                        matched_container_id
                    )
                    VALUES (
                        :cycle_id,
                        :raw_code,
                        :barcode,
                        :matched_container_id
                    )
                """), {
                    "cycle_id": cycle_id,
                    "raw_code": barcode,   # <-- THIS FIX
                    "barcode": barcode,
                    "matched_container_id": matched_container_id
                })
                if matched_container_id:
                    matched += 1

                    conn.execute(text("""
                        INSERT INTO container_scans (
                            container_id,
                            cycle_id,
                            barcode,
                            source,
                            status
                        )
                        VALUES (
                            :container_id,
                            :cycle_id,
                            :barcode,
                            'UPLOAD',
                            'FOUND'
                        )
                    """), {
                        "container_id": matched_container_id,
                        "cycle_id": cycle_id,
                        "barcode": barcode
                    })

                    conn.execute(text("""
                        UPDATE containers
                        SET last_scan_at = NOW()
                        WHERE container_id = :container_id
                    """), {
                        "container_id": matched_container_id
                    })
                else:
                    unmatched += 1

            conn.execute(text("""
                UPDATE inventory_cycles
                SET matched_count = :matched,
                    unmatched_count = :unmatched
                WHERE cycle_id = :cycle_id
            """), {
                "matched": matched,
                "unmatched": unmatched,
                "cycle_id": cycle_id
            })
            self.log_transaction(
                    conn,
                    action="SCAN_UPLOAD",
                    performed_by=performed_by,
                    details={
                        "cycle_id": cycle_id,
                        "report_name": report_name,
                        "location": location,
                        "filename": filename,
                        "total_scanned": total,
                        "matched_count": matched,
                        "unmatched_count": unmatched,
                        "notes": report_name
                    }
                )
        return {
            "cycle_id": cycle_id,
            "total": total,
            "matched": matched,
            "unmatched": unmatched,
        }

    def get_barcode_queue(self, query="", only_unprinted="1", limit=500):
        """Get barcode queue with optional filtering"""
        where = []
        params = {}

        if only_unprinted == "1":
            where.append("COALESCE(c.label_printed, FALSE) = FALSE")

        if query:
            where.append("""
                (
                    COALESCE(c.barcode,'')        ILIKE :q OR
                    COALESCE(i.name,'')           ILIKE :q OR
                    COALESCE(i.catalog_number,'') ILIKE :q OR
                    COALESCE(c.lot_number,'')     ILIKE :q OR
                    COALESCE(r.room_no,'')        ILIKE :q OR
                    COALESCE(r.room_desc,'')      ILIKE :q
                )
            """)
            params["q"] = f"%{query}%"

        where_sql = ("WHERE " + " AND ".join(where)) if where else ""

        sql = f"""
            SELECT
                c.container_id,
                c.barcode,
                c.created_at AS created_at,
                COALESCE(i.name, i.description)      AS item_name,
                i.catalog_number,
                c.lot_number,
                COALESCE(c.label_printed, FALSE)     AS label_printed,
                r.room_no,
                r.room_desc
            FROM containers c
            JOIN items i   ON i.item_id  = c.item_id
            LEFT JOIN rooms r ON r.room_id = c.room_id
            {where_sql}
            ORDER BY c.created_at DESC NULLS LAST, c.container_id DESC
            LIMIT :lim
        """
        params["lim"] = limit

        with self.engine.begin() as conn:
            rows = conn.execute(text(sql), params).mappings().all()

        return rows

    def get_barcode_labels(self, query="", copies=1, limit=1000):
        """Get barcode labels for printing"""
        where = []
        params = {"lim": limit}

        if query:
            where.append("""
                (
                    COALESCE(i.name,'') ILIKE :q OR
                    COALESCE(c.barcode,'') ILIKE :q OR
                    COALESCE(r.room_no,'') ILIKE :q OR
                    COALESCE(r.room_desc,'') ILIKE :q
                )
            """)
            params["q"] = f"%{query}%"

        where_sql = "WHERE " + " AND ".join(where) if where else ""

        sql = f"""
            SELECT
                COALESCE(i.name, i.description) AS item_name,
                c.lot_number,
                c.barcode AS barcode_number
            FROM containers c
            JOIN items i   ON i.item_id  = c.item_id
            LEFT JOIN rooms r ON r.room_id = c.room_id
            {where_sql}
            ORDER BY c.container_id
            LIMIT :lim
        """

        with self.engine.begin() as conn:
            rows = conn.execute(text(sql), params).mappings().all()

        # Apply copies
        labels = []
        for r in rows:
            for _ in range(copies):
                labels.append({
                    "item_name": r["item_name"],
                    "lot_number": r["lot_number"],
                    "barcode_number": r["barcode_number"],
                })

        return labels

    def export_inventory_csv(self, query="", limit=500000):
        rows = self.search_inventory(query, limit, show_removed=True)
        if not rows:
            return "No data"
        import csv
        import io
        output = io.StringIO()
        writer = csv.DictWriter(output, fieldnames=rows[0].keys())
        writer.writeheader()
        for row in rows:
            writer.writerow(dict(row))
        return output.getvalue()

#REMOVE CONTAINER updated 4/16/2026
    def remove_container(self, barcode, removed_by=None, reason=None, notes=None):
        from sqlalchemy import text

        def clean_str(value):
            if value is None:
                return None
            value = str(value).strip()
            return value if value else None

        barcode = clean_str(barcode)
        removed_by = clean_str(removed_by)
        reason = clean_str(reason)
        notes = clean_str(notes)

        with self.engine.begin() as conn:
            current = conn.execute(text("""
                SELECT
                    container_id,
                    item_id,
                    room_id,
                    barcode,
                    notes
                FROM containers
                WHERE TRIM(barcode) = :bc
                  AND COALESCE(status, 'ACTIVE') != 'REMOVED'
                LIMIT 1
            """), {"bc": barcode}).mappings().first()

            if not current:
                return False

            existing_notes = current["notes"] or ""
            removal_note = "Removed"
            if reason:
                removal_note += f": {reason}"
            if notes:
                removal_note += f" {notes}"

            combined_notes = existing_notes.strip()
            if combined_notes:
                combined_notes += "\n" + removal_note
            else:
                combined_notes = removal_note

            conn.execute(text("""
                UPDATE containers
                SET
                    status = 'REMOVED',
                    notes = :notes
                WHERE container_id = :cid
            """), {
                "notes": combined_notes,
                "cid": current["container_id"]
            })

            self.log_transaction(
                conn,
                action="REMOVE",
                container_id=current["container_id"],
                barcode=current["barcode"],
                item_id=current["item_id"],
                room_id=current["room_id"],
                performed_by=removed_by,
                details={
                    "reason": reason or None,
                    "notes": notes or None,
                    "status": "REMOVED"
                }
            )

            return True
#Added 4/20/2026 Bulk remove containers wrapper
    def remove_containers_by_barcodes(self, raw_barcodes, removed_by=None, reason=None, notes=None):
        def clean_str(value):
            if value is None:
                return None
            value = str(value).strip()
            return value if value else None

        def parse_barcodes(raw):
            if not raw:
                return []
            raw = str(raw).replace(",", "\n").replace("\t", "\n").replace("\r", "\n")
            seen = set()
            out = []
            for line in raw.split("\n"):
                bc = line.strip().replace(" ", "")
                if not bc:
                    continue
                if bc not in seen:
                    seen.add(bc)
                    out.append(bc)
            return out

        removed_by = clean_str(removed_by)
        reason = clean_str(reason)
        notes = clean_str(notes)

        barcodes = parse_barcodes(raw_barcodes)

        removed = []
        not_found = []

        for bc in barcodes:
            ok = self.remove_container(
                barcode=bc,
                removed_by=removed_by,
                reason=reason,
                notes=notes,
            )
            if ok:
                removed.append(bc)
            else:
                not_found.append(bc)

        return {
            "requested_count": len(barcodes),
            "removed_count": len(removed),
            "removed": removed,
            "not_found": not_found,
        }


#Move container fixed 4/16/2026
    def move_container(
        self,
        barcode,
        room_no,
        room_desc,
        area_class,
        storage_location,
        storage_sublocation,
        storage_device,
        moved_by=None
    ):
        from sqlalchemy import text

        def clean_str(value):
            if value is None:
                return None
            value = str(value).strip()
            return value if value else None

        barcode = clean_str(barcode)
        room_no = clean_str(room_no)
        room_desc = clean_str(room_desc)
        area_class = clean_str(area_class)
        storage_location = clean_str(storage_location)
        storage_sublocation = clean_str(storage_sublocation)
        storage_device = clean_str(storage_device)
        moved_by = clean_str(moved_by)

        with self.engine.begin() as conn:
            current = conn.execute(text("""
                SELECT
                    container_id,
                    item_id,
                    room_id,
                    barcode,
                    storage_location,
                    storage_sublocation,
                    storage_device
                FROM containers
                WHERE TRIM(barcode) = :bc
                  AND COALESCE(status, 'ACTIVE') != 'REMOVED'
                LIMIT 1
            """), {"bc": barcode}).mappings().first()

            if not current:
                return False

            new_room_id = self.resolve_room_id(conn, room_no, room_desc, area_class)

            old_room_id = current["room_id"]
            old_storage_location = current["storage_location"]
            old_storage_sublocation = current["storage_sublocation"]
            old_storage_device = current["storage_device"]

            conn.execute(text("""
                UPDATE containers
                SET
                    room_id = COALESCE(:room_id, room_id),
                    area_class = COALESCE(:area_class, area_class),
                    storage_location = COALESCE(:sloc, storage_location),
                    storage_sublocation = COALESCE(:ssub, storage_sublocation),
                    storage_device = COALESCE(:sdev, storage_device)
                WHERE container_id = :cid
            """), {
                "room_id": new_room_id,
                "area_class": area_class,
                "sloc": storage_location,
                "ssub": storage_sublocation,
                "sdev": storage_device,
                "cid": current["container_id"],
            })

            self.log_transaction(
                conn,
                action="MOVE",
                container_id=current["container_id"],
                barcode=current["barcode"],
                item_id=current["item_id"],
                room_id=new_room_id,
                performed_by=moved_by,
                details={
                    "from_room_id": old_room_id,
                    "to_room_id": new_room_id,
                    "from_storage_location": old_storage_location,
                    "to_storage_location": storage_location,
                    "from_storage_sublocation": old_storage_sublocation,
                    "to_storage_sublocation": storage_sublocation,
                    "from_storage_device": old_storage_device,
                    "to_storage_device": storage_device,
                    "notes": "Move"
                }
            )

            return True
#Bulk Move Barcodes 4/15/2026
    def bulk_move_by_barcodes(
        self,
        raw_barcodes,
        room_no=None,
        room_desc=None,
        area_class=None,
        storage_location=None,
        storage_sublocation=None,
        storage_device=None,
        performed_by=None,
    ):
        from sqlalchemy import text

        def clean_str(value):
            if value is None:
                return None
            value = str(value).strip()
            return value if value else None

        def parse_barcodes(raw):
            if not raw:
                return []
            raw = str(raw).replace(",", "\n").replace("\t", "\n").replace("\r", "\n")
            seen = set()
            out = []
            for line in raw.split("\n"):
                bc = line.strip().replace(" ", "")
                if not bc:
                    continue
                if bc not in seen:
                    seen.add(bc)
                    out.append(bc)
            return out

        barcodes = parse_barcodes(raw_barcodes)

        print("RAW BULK INPUT:", repr(raw_barcodes))
        print("PARSED BARCODES:", barcodes)

        if not barcodes:
            return {
                "requested_count": 0,
                "matched_count": 0,
                "moved_count": 0,
                "unmatched": [],
            }

        room_no = clean_str(room_no)
        room_desc = clean_str(room_desc)
        area_class = clean_str(area_class)
        storage_location = clean_str(storage_location)
        storage_sublocation = clean_str(storage_sublocation)
        storage_device = clean_str(storage_device)
        performed_by = clean_str(performed_by)

        print("DESTINATION:", {
            "room_no": room_no,
            "room_desc": room_desc,
            "area_class": area_class,
            "storage_location": storage_location,
            "storage_sublocation": storage_sublocation,
            "storage_device": storage_device,
            "performed_by": performed_by,
        })

        if not (room_no or room_desc or area_class or storage_location or storage_sublocation or storage_device):
            return {
                "requested_count": len(barcodes),
                "matched_count": 0,
                "moved_count": 0,
                "unmatched": [],
            }

        moved_count = 0
        unmatched = []

        with self.engine.begin() as conn:
            new_room_id = self.resolve_room_id(conn, room_no, room_desc, area_class)
            print("RESOLVED ROOM ID:", new_room_id)

            for bc in barcodes:
                print("TRYING BARCODE:", repr(bc))

                current = conn.execute(text("""
                    SELECT
                        container_id,
                        item_id,
                        room_id,
                        barcode,
                        storage_location,
                        storage_sublocation,
                        storage_device
                    FROM containers
                    WHERE TRIM(barcode) = :bc
                      AND COALESCE(status, 'ACTIVE') != 'REMOVED'
                    LIMIT 1
                """), {"bc": bc}).mappings().first()

                if not current:
                    unmatched.append(bc)
                    continue

                old_room_id = current["room_id"]
                old_storage_location = current["storage_location"]
                old_storage_sublocation = current["storage_sublocation"]
                old_storage_device = current["storage_device"]

                res = conn.execute(text("""
                    UPDATE containers
                    SET
                        room_id = COALESCE(:room_id, room_id),
                        area_class = COALESCE(:area_class, area_class),
                        storage_location = COALESCE(:sloc, storage_location),
                        storage_sublocation = COALESCE(:ssub, storage_sublocation),
                        storage_device = COALESCE(:sdev, storage_device)
                    WHERE container_id = :container_id
                    RETURNING container_id
                """), {
                    "room_id": new_room_id,
                    "area_class": area_class,
                    "sloc": storage_location,
                    "ssub": storage_sublocation,
                    "sdev": storage_device,
                    "container_id": current["container_id"],
                }).scalar()

                if res:
                    moved_count += 1

                    self.log_transaction(
                        conn,
                        action="BULK_MOVE",
                        container_id=current["container_id"],
                        barcode=current["barcode"],
                        item_id=current["item_id"],
                        room_id=new_room_id,
                        performed_by=performed_by,
                        details={
                            "from_room_id": old_room_id,
                            "to_room_id": new_room_id,
                            "from_storage_location": old_storage_location,
                            "to_storage_location": storage_location,
                            "from_storage_sublocation": old_storage_sublocation,
                            "to_storage_sublocation": storage_sublocation,
                            "from_storage_device": old_storage_device,
                            "to_storage_device": storage_device,
                            "notes": "Bulk move"
                        }
                    )
                else:
                    unmatched.append(bc)

        return {
            "requested_count": len(barcodes),
            "matched_count": moved_count,
            "moved_count": moved_count,
            "unmatched": unmatched,
        }
#EDIT/UPDATE CONTAINER UPDATED 4/16/2026
    def update_container(self, container_id, data):
        from sqlalchemy import text

        def keep_or_update(new, old):
            new = (new or "").strip()
            return old if new == "" else new

        with self.engine.begin() as conn:
            current = conn.execute(text("""
                SELECT
                    item_id,
                    room_id,
                    manuf_date,
                    expiry_date,
                    nmr_expiry,
                    storage_location,
                    storage_sublocation,
                    storage_device,
                    size,
                    unit,
                    system,
                    lot_number,
                    choice,
                    nmr,
                    owner,
                    notes,
                    barcode
                FROM containers
                WHERE container_id = :cid
            """), {"cid": container_id}).mappings().first()

            if not current:
                raise ValueError(f"Container {container_id} not found")

            new_name = (data.get("name") or "").strip()
            current_item_id = current["item_id"]
            new_name = (
                data.get("name")
                or data.get("material_name")
                or data.get("item_name")
                or data.get("chemical_name")
                or ""
            ).strip()

            if new_name:
                conn.execute(text("""
                    UPDATE items
                    SET name = :name,
                        description = :name
                    WHERE item_id = :item_id
                """), {
                    "name": new_name,
                    "item_id": current["item_id"]
                })
            room_id = self.resolve_room_id(
                conn,
                data.get("room_no"),
                data.get("room_desc"),
                data.get("area_class")
            )

            manuf = keep_or_update(data.get("manuf_date"), current["manuf_date"])
            exp = keep_or_update(data.get("expire"), current["expiry_date"])
            nmr_exp = keep_or_update(data.get("nmr_exp"), current["nmr_expiry"])

            sloc = keep_or_update(data.get("storage_location"), current["storage_location"])
            ssub = keep_or_update(data.get("storage_subloc"), current["storage_sublocation"])
            sdev = keep_or_update(data.get("storage_device"), current["storage_device"])
            size = keep_or_update(data.get("size"), current["size"])
            unit = keep_or_update(data.get("unit"), current["unit"])
            sys = keep_or_update(data.get("system"), current["system"])
            lot = keep_or_update(data.get("lot_number"), current["lot_number"])
            choice = keep_or_update(data.get("choice"), current["choice"])
            nmr = keep_or_update(data.get("nmr"), current["nmr"])
            owner = keep_or_update(data.get("owner"), current["owner"])
            notes = keep_or_update(data.get("notes"), current["notes"])

            conn.execute(text("""
                UPDATE containers
                SET room_id = :room_id,
                    storage_location = :sloc,
                    storage_sublocation = :ssub,
                    storage_device = :sdev,
                    size = :size,
                    unit = :unit,
                    system = :sys,
                    manuf_date = :manuf,
                    expiry_date = :exp,
                    lot_number = :lot,
                    choice = :choice,
                    nmr = :nmr,
                    nmr_expiry = :nmr_exp,
                    owner = :owner,
                    notes = :notes
                WHERE container_id = :cid
            """), {
                "room_id": room_id,
                "sloc": sloc,
                "ssub": ssub,
                "sdev": sdev,
                "size": size,
                "unit": unit,
                "sys": sys,
                "manuf": manuf,
                "exp": exp,
                "lot": lot,
                "choice": choice,
                "nmr": nmr,
                "nmr_exp": nmr_exp,
                "owner": owner,
                "notes": notes,
                "cid": container_id
            })

            updated_fields = {
                "material_name": new_name if new_name else None,
                "room_id": room_id,
                "storage_location": sloc,
                "storage_sublocation": ssub,
                "storage_device": sdev,
                "size": size,
                "unit": unit,
                "system": sys,
                "manuf_date": str(manuf) if manuf else None,
                "expiry_date": str(exp) if exp else None,
                "lot_number": lot,
                "choice": choice,
                "nmr": nmr,
                "nmr_expiry": str(nmr_exp) if nmr_exp else None,
                "owner": owner,
                "notes": notes
            }

            self.log_transaction(
                conn,
                action="EDIT",
                container_id=container_id,
                barcode=current["barcode"],
                item_id=current["item_id"],
                room_id=room_id,
                performed_by=data.get("performed_by") or data.get("added_by") or None,
                details={
                    "notes": notes,
                    "updated_fields": updated_fields
                }
            )
#GET TRANSACTIONS 4/16/2026
    def get_transactions(self, q="", limit=500):
        from sqlalchemy import text

        q = (q or "").strip()
        like = f"%{q}%"

        sql = """
            SELECT
                t.transaction_id,
                t.action,
                t.container_id,
                t.barcode,
                t.item_id,
                t.room_id,
                t.details,
                t.performed_by,
                t.created_at,

                i.name AS material_name,
                r.room_no,
                c.storage_location,

                COALESCE(t.details::json->>'reason', '') AS reason,
                COALESCE(t.details::json->>'notes', c.notes, '') AS notes

            FROM transactions t
            LEFT JOIN containers c ON t.container_id = c.container_id
            LEFT JOIN items i ON COALESCE(t.item_id, c.item_id) = i.item_id
            LEFT JOIN rooms r ON COALESCE(t.room_id, c.room_id) = r.room_id
            WHERE 1=1
        """

        params = {"limit": limit}

        if q:
            sql += """
                AND (
                    COALESCE(t.action, '') ILIKE :like
                    OR COALESCE(t.barcode, '') ILIKE :like
                    OR COALESCE(t.performed_by, '') ILIKE :like
                    OR COALESCE(t.details, '') ILIKE :like
                    OR COALESCE(i.name, '') ILIKE :like
                    OR COALESCE(r.room_no, '') ILIKE :like
                    OR COALESCE(c.storage_location, '') ILIKE :like
                )
            """
            params["like"] = like

        sql += """
            ORDER BY t.created_at DESC, t.transaction_id DESC
            LIMIT :limit
        """

        with self.engine.begin() as conn:
            rows = conn.execute(text(sql), params).mappings().all()

        return rows

    def suggest(self, field, q, limit=10):
        # Stub implementation
        return []

    def autofill(self, catalog="", name=""):
        # Stub implementation
        return {}

    def mark_barcodes_printed(self, barcodes):
        """Mark barcodes as printed"""
        with self.engine.begin() as conn:
            result = conn.execute(
                text("""
                    UPDATE containers
                    SET label_printed = TRUE,
                        label_printed_at = NOW()
                    WHERE barcode = ANY(:bcs)
                """),
                {"bcs": barcodes}
            )
            return result.rowcount
#Scan services 4/15/2026

    def get_scan_reports(self, limit=200):
        from sqlalchemy import text

        with self.engine.begin() as conn:
            rows = conn.execute(text("""
                SELECT
                    cycle_id,
                    COALESCE(report_name, 'Unnamed Scan Report') AS report_name,
                    COALESCE(performed_by, '') AS performed_by,
                    COALESCE(location, '') AS location,
                    COALESCE(filename, '') AS filename,
                    COALESCE(total_scanned, 0) AS total_scanned,
                    COALESCE(matched_count, 0) AS matched_count,
                    COALESCE(unmatched_count, 0) AS unmatched_count,
                    created_at
                FROM inventory_cycles
                ORDER BY cycle_id DESC
                LIMIT :limit
            """), {"limit": limit}).mappings().all()

        return rows

    def get_inventory_scan_coverage(self, limit=5000):
        from sqlalchemy import text

        with self.engine.begin() as conn:
            rows = conn.execute(text("""
                SELECT
                    c.container_id,
                    c.barcode,
                    i.name AS material_name,
                    i.catalog_number,
                    r.room_no,
                    r.room_name,
                    c.area_class,
                    c.storage_location,
                    c.storage_sublocation,
                    c.storage_device,
                    c.owner,
                    c.last_scan_at,
                    CASE
                        WHEN c.last_scan_at IS NULL THEN 'UNSCANNED'
                        ELSE 'SCANNED'
                    END AS scan_status
                FROM containers c
                LEFT JOIN items i ON c.item_id = i.item_id
                LEFT JOIN rooms r ON c.room_id = r.room_id
                WHERE COALESCE(c.status, 'ACTIVE') != 'REMOVED'
                ORDER BY
                    CASE WHEN c.last_scan_at IS NULL THEN 0 ELSE 1 END,
                    r.room_no NULLS LAST,
                    i.name NULLS LAST,
                    c.barcode NULLS LAST
                LIMIT :limit
            """), {"limit": limit}).mappings().all()

        return rows
#Report Services Added 4/15/2026
    def report_totals(self):
        from sqlalchemy import text

        with self.engine.begin() as conn:
            row = conn.execute(text("""
                SELECT
                    COUNT(*) AS total_containers,
                    COUNT(DISTINCT item_id) AS unique_materials,
                    COUNT(*) FILTER (
                        WHERE expiry_date IS NOT NULL
                          AND expiry_date >= CURRENT_DATE
                          AND expiry_date <= CURRENT_DATE + INTERVAL '30 days'
                    ) AS expiring_30,
                    COUNT(*) FILTER (
                        WHERE expiry_date IS NOT NULL
                          AND expiry_date < CURRENT_DATE
                    ) AS expired
                FROM containers
                WHERE COALESCE(status, 'ACTIVE') != 'REMOVED'
            """)).mappings().first()

        return row or {
            "total_containers": 0,
            "unique_materials": 0,
            "expiring_30": 0,
            "expired": 0,
        }

    def report_expiring(self):
        from sqlalchemy import text

        with self.engine.begin() as conn:
            rows = conn.execute(text("""
                SELECT
                    c.expiry_date AS exp_date,
                    i.name AS material_name,
                    c.size,
                    c.unit,
                    v.vendor_name AS vendor,
                    c.lot_number,
                    r.room_no,
                    r.room_name AS room_desc,
                    c.storage_location,
                    c.storage_sublocation,
                    c.owner,
                    c.barcode
                FROM containers c
                LEFT JOIN items i ON c.item_id = i.item_id
                LEFT JOIN vendors v ON i.vendor_id = v.vendor_id
                LEFT JOIN rooms r ON c.room_id = r.room_id
                WHERE COALESCE(c.status, 'ACTIVE') != 'REMOVED'
                  AND c.expiry_date IS NOT NULL
                  AND c.expiry_date >= CURRENT_DATE
                  AND c.expiry_date <= CURRENT_DATE + INTERVAL '30 days'
                ORDER BY c.expiry_date ASC, i.name ASC
            """)).mappings().all()

        return rows

    def report_expired(self):
        from sqlalchemy import text

        with self.engine.begin() as conn:
            rows = conn.execute(text("""
                SELECT
                    c.expiry_date AS exp_date,
                    i.name AS material_name,
                    c.size,
                    c.unit,
                    v.vendor_name AS vendor,
                    c.lot_number,
                    r.room_no,
                    r.room_name AS room_desc,
                    c.storage_location,
                    c.storage_sublocation,
                    c.owner,
                    c.barcode
                FROM containers c
                LEFT JOIN items i ON c.item_id = i.item_id
                LEFT JOIN vendors v ON i.vendor_id = v.vendor_id
                LEFT JOIN rooms r ON c.room_id = r.room_id
                WHERE COALESCE(c.status, 'ACTIVE') != 'REMOVED'
                  AND c.expiry_date IS NOT NULL
                  AND c.expiry_date < CURRENT_DATE
                ORDER BY c.expiry_date ASC, i.name ASC
            """)).mappings().all()

        return rows

    def report_nmr_due(self):
        from sqlalchemy import text

        with self.engine.begin() as conn:
            rows = conn.execute(text("""
                SELECT
                    c.nmr_expiry AS nmr_exp,
                    c.nmr,
                    i.name AS material_name,
                    c.owner,
                    r.room_no,
                    r.room_name AS room_desc,
                    c.barcode
                FROM containers c
                LEFT JOIN items i ON c.item_id = i.item_id
                LEFT JOIN rooms r ON c.room_id = r.room_id
                WHERE COALESCE(c.status, 'ACTIVE') != 'REMOVED'
                  AND c.nmr_expiry IS NOT NULL
                  AND c.nmr_expiry <= CURRENT_DATE + INTERVAL '30 days'
                ORDER BY c.nmr_expiry ASC, i.name ASC
            """)).mappings().all()

        return rows

    def report_by_room(self):
        from sqlalchemy import text

        with self.engine.begin() as conn:
            rows = conn.execute(text("""
                SELECT
                    COALESCE(r.room_no, '') AS room_no,
                    COALESCE(r.room_name, '') AS room_desc,
                    COUNT(*) AS n
                FROM containers c
                LEFT JOIN rooms r ON c.room_id = r.room_id
                WHERE COALESCE(c.status, 'ACTIVE') != 'REMOVED'
                GROUP BY r.room_no, r.room_name
                ORDER BY r.room_no NULLS LAST, r.room_name NULLS LAST
            """)).mappings().all()

        return rows

    def report_by_vendor(self):
        from sqlalchemy import text

        with self.engine.begin() as conn:
            rows = conn.execute(text("""
                SELECT
                    COALESCE(v.vendor_name, '') AS vendor,
                    COUNT(*) AS n
                FROM containers c
                LEFT JOIN items i ON c.item_id = i.item_id
                LEFT JOIN vendors v ON i.vendor_id = v.vendor_id
                WHERE COALESCE(c.status, 'ACTIVE') != 'REMOVED'
                GROUP BY v.vendor_name
                ORDER BY COUNT(*) DESC, v.vendor_name
            """)).mappings().all()

        return rows

    def report_by_system(self):
        from sqlalchemy import text

        with self.engine.begin() as conn:
            rows = conn.execute(text("""
                SELECT
                    COALESCE(c.system, '') AS system,
                    COUNT(*) AS n
                FROM containers c
                WHERE COALESCE(c.status, 'ACTIVE') != 'REMOVED'
                GROUP BY c.system
                ORDER BY COUNT(*) DESC, c.system
            """)).mappings().all()

        return rows

    def report_by_owner(self):
        from sqlalchemy import text

        with self.engine.begin() as conn:
            rows = conn.execute(text("""
                SELECT
                    COALESCE(c.owner, '') AS owner,
                    COUNT(*) AS n
                FROM containers c
                WHERE COALESCE(c.status, 'ACTIVE') != 'REMOVED'
                GROUP BY c.owner
                ORDER BY COUNT(*) DESC, c.owner
            """)).mappings().all()

        return rows

#4/15/2026 Log transcation new
    def log_transaction(
        self,
        conn,
        action,
        container_id=None,
        barcode=None,
        item_id=None,
        room_id=None,
        details=None,
        performed_by=None
    ):
        from sqlalchemy import text
        import json

        conn.execute(text("""
            INSERT INTO transactions (
                action,
                container_id,
                barcode,
                item_id,
                room_id,
                details,
                performed_by,
                created_at
            )
            VALUES (
                :action,
                :container_id,
                :barcode,
                :item_id,
                :room_id,
                :details,
                :performed_by,
                NOW()
            )
        """), {
            "action": action,
            "container_id": container_id,
            "barcode": barcode,
            "item_id": item_id,
            "room_id": room_id,
            "details": json.dumps(details or {}),
            "performed_by": performed_by
        })
```
